< text>
Jack & Charlie's is in the basement of Visalia old jail house. It's quaint like something out of the roaring 20's except in today's standards. There's a red rose or red carnation on each table and you are seated at a table with white table cloth with nice silverware place settings and cloth napkins. It's very classy and brings you back to an era that has been long gone.
Service is very good and the food is good. They do have a bar area that makes fantastic drinks.< /text>

Afterwards, we had their Mac N Cheese again, and everything was delivered on point. My wife and I both had their Filet Minon. I had their four-course meal, all of my servings was outstanding, as well as my wife‚Äôs.

Original Post: My wife and I came here 8/9/19, excited as we had tried Vintage Press and The Depot, both were terrific. We arrived around 7:15 PM, and were seated in the bar area because it was pretty busy. It took at least 10 minutes to get drinks ordered. Then after we had our drinks for another 10-15 minutes, our waitress came and took our order, she had intended just for us to order an appetizer, however we wanted to our food ordered since we could see things were taking a bit longer. After we waited for another 20 minutes, our appetizer, MAC and cheese was delivered, which was delicious. After we had finished, we waited another 30 minutes for our dinner to finally arrive. We were offered another round of drinks after our appetizer was finished, which we agreed, however those didn‚Äôt show up until after our dinner had been served. We also found it incredibly rude that our waitress had time to talk to people she knew personally, talking about texting them and going on about their personal lives, as our service had been pretty poor, along with our food.

<review>I can't believe there are no reviews for Jack and Charlie's!!! This is one of our favorite restaurants in Visalia. Classic, but basic, art nouveau design. If you are looking for true exciting, creative, market-fresh bistro-syle food, this is your place. Think Wolfgang Puck in the early days. I could go on and on about favorite dishes we have had there--unique appetizers that you won't find anywhere (I don't care where you go), foie gras, great fish dishes (depending on what is fresh), beef stroganoff made with steak and fresh noodles, steaks, fabulous bread pudding. Specially selected wines, unique bar drinks and a specialty in absinthes. Great bar scene. I hesitate to tell you how good this place really is as I selfishly don't want everyone to go.... The only disappointment about this restaurant is the menu sometimes changes---as it must---but the excitement of trying new dishes typically makes up for it.<//review><Date>1559037978370<//Date><user>115360496187310813108</user><Response>None< /Response>< Name>

My fiance and I came here for dinner and it was the best experience and great tasting food I've had in a while. A small example of the service: they led us to our booth with menus and let us look over it.....we noticed the glasses on the table had water spots on them...the server came back and noticed as well. Would definitely recommend and look forward to going again.<//Text>

< text>
This little spot is great.   I absolutely hate having to work in Hanford, CA so I usually drive out 20 minutes or so to Visalia to stay.   This is one of my go to spots in the cool little down town area.  The food is great, however, I do order the same thing every time.   Beef, Filet Mignon (California) Roasted Fingerling Potatoes, Shaved Zucchini, Cognac, Green Peppercorns 39... its fantastic and they give you bone marrow butter on the side.   Cant go wrong and some great local beer choices as well. No 805, but no point deducted.  Look for the red phone booth and head downstairs for a real treat.</text>

<UserId.>108882219736704250550</UserId.><user_name>Keddy Lichaadzohn< /user_name><date>1513020199302< /date><rate>5< /rate>< Review>
UPDATE : This is an authentic Mexican restaurant. I noticed in a Google search of Mexican restaurants in the area that this did not show up. Hopefully mentioning this now will help.

My kids and I were very sad to see the old Cotixan go. Although their food wasn't necessarily amazing or consistent, their carne / carnitas / Cali burritos and chimis were our go-to comfort food for years.

LUCKILY, Chamoy Taqueria + Fruteria just opened up to replace the old taco shop, and Poway is all the better for it! Our first visit was tonight just to check things out, although it's been open since late November. The decor has been completely redone and has a more colorful and friendly vibe with big food posters and banda music playing. You'll immediately notice boxes and fridge displays of fresh fruit near the front containing all sorts of tropical - ish varieties... Especially mangoes. Lots and LOTS of mangoes. All of this highlights this restaurant's emphasis on fresh fruit menu items... And there's a LOT on the menu. (See the menu pics)

The food... All kinds of fresh fruit items plus your standard So Cal taco shop menu offerings, along with some unique and trendy items like the quesaburrito and churros locos. I did order the quesaburrito because their description of having 'crunchy cheese' inside caught my attention. It had absolutely no crunch whatsoever, but it was a pretty darn good version of a carne asada burrito. It had a nice flavor and lots of fresh guac. They also didn't disappoint on the size, which was as big as most folks' forearms.

I also had a big mango agua fresca, which was outstanding. They were extremely generous with the fresh mangoes, and I could almost chew on my drink with every sip. Delicious! I can't wait to come back and try some different things in the very near future.< /Review>
